      document.write('<DIV style="POSITION: relative; TOP: -4px; LEFT: 0px; HEIGHT: 77px;"><A href="http://www5.samsclub.com/InClubsNow.aspx?iid=TDR1"><IMG title="In Clubs Now" alt="In Clubs Now" src="http://www.samsclub.com/sams/en_US/images/icn-CartRailBanner.png"></A></DIV><DIV style="height:33px; line-height:33px;"><img src="http://www.samsclub.com/sams/images/bg-blueBar.gif"></DIV>');
      OAS_AD('x69');
    }
    else 
    {      
      document.write('');
    }    
  }
  else 
  {      
    document.write('');
  }
}
//  End -->
</SCRIPT>

// WWW8.SAMSCLUB.COM to WWW.CELLSTORES.COM workaround - TEMPORARY
// update all a href's from www8.samsclub.com to www.cellstores.com
$('a').ready(function(){$('a[href*="www8.samsclub.com"]').each(function(){$(this).attr('href',$(this).attr('href').replace('www8.samsclub.com','www.cellstores.com'));});});
// catch the meta redirect and throw another redirect before it fires
$('meta').ready(function(){if($('meta[content*="www8.samsclub.com"]').length>0){setTimeout(function(){document.location.href=$('meta[content*="www8.samsclub.com"]').attr('content').substr(6).replace('www8.samsclub.com','www.cellstores.com');},200);}});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery.fn.tooltip=function(content,fade,pause){if(content == 'title'){content=$(this).attr('title');}$(this).attr('title','');if(fade!=parseInt(fade)){fade=200;}if(pause!=parseInt(pause)){pause=250;}tolink=$(this);var tooltipattached=false;var totimeout;tolink.hover(function(){if(tooltipattached==false){$(this).append('<div class="tooltip"><p>'+content+'</p></div>');tooltipattached=true;}$(this).children('.tooltip').stop(true,true).fadeIn(fade);clearTimeout(totimeout);},function(){var $tooltip=$(this).children('.tooltip');totimeout=setTimeout(function(){$tooltip.stop(true,true).fadeOut(fade);},pause);});};
</script>

			function replaceSquo(value){
				if(value.length > 0) {
				value = value.replace(/&lt;/g,"<");
				value = value.replace(/&gt;/g,">");
				value = value.replace(/&amp;/g,"&");
				value = value.replace(/&#039;/g,"'");
				value = value.replace(/&#034;/g,'"');
				value = value.replace(/&#39;/g,"'");
				value = value.replace(/&#34;/g,'"');
				value = value.replace(/&quot;/g,'"');
				value =	value.replace(/&rsquo;/g,"'");
				}
				return value;
			}
